        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1042374532" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18295324845915967478">Also reviewed for <a href='http://www.addicted2heroines.com/2014/09/review-up-from-grave-night-huntress-7.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Addicted2Heroines</a>.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>After 10 or 15 pages, my only thought was this:</b>
</i><br/><b>I hope this series ends soon.</b><br/><br/>Yep.<br/>Evidently, I was the only person on earth who didn't realize that <i>this</i> <b>is</b> the last book in the series.<br/>Whoops.<br/>Ok. Well, good for Jeaniene Frost! I hate to say it, because I fell in love with these characters <i>years</i> ago, but I was just about burned out on Cat & Bones.<br/><i>
  <b>Gasp! Sacrilege!</b>
</i><br/>No. I don't mean it like that. What I mean is, I'm glad that <i>for once</i> an author didn't milk a s</span>
  <span id="freeText18295324845915967478" style="display:none">Also reviewed for <a href="http://www.addicted2heroines.com/2014/09/review-up-from-grave-night-huntress-7.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted2Heroines</a>.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>After 10 or 15 pages, my only thought was this:</b>
</i><br /><b>I hope this series ends soon.</b><br /><br />Yep.<br />Evidently, I was the only person on earth who didn't realize that <i>this</i> <b>is</b> the last book in the series.<br />Whoops.<br />Ok. Well, good for Jeaniene Frost! I hate to say it, because I fell in love with these characters <i>years</i> ago, but I was just about burned out on Cat &amp; Bones.<br /><i>
  <b>Gasp! Sacrilege!</b>
</i><br />No. I don't mean it like that. What I mean is, I'm glad that <i>for once</i> an author didn't milk a series until it was drier than a dead cow's tit.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Hi Charlaine! How's the Sam &amp; Sookie fan club these days? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I'm not going to bother with spoilers, but I will say I'm basically happy with the send-off that Frost gave these guys.<br />There was no way for this to end in some absolutely glorious way...that <b>everyone</b> would love...but I think she came pretty close.<br />So, for that alone, I would give this book 4 stars.<br />But, luckily, it isn't just getting pity stars from me.<br />It had enough fun Cat 'n Bones stuff in it to keep my interest for the entire book. Lots of old characters made an impact on the story, and a couple of new characters kept it fresh.<br /><br />It wasn't a 5 star read for me, though.<br />I never felt any <i>real</i> fear for any of the characters that were supposedly in <b>danger</b>. The <i>twists</i> were surprisingly easy to see coming, and without any shocking Reveals, it didn't quite pack the punch that would land it in 5 star territory for me.<br /><br />Still, it was a good ending to one of the first paranormal series that I fell in love with.<br />Overall, very well done!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer7755359368284985489">Don contacts Cat & Bones when he can't find or reach his old team (Tate, Juan, Dave and Cooper). They've been out of communication for weeks so it doesn't take long for them to connect their disappearance to Madigan. With the assistance of Ian, Spade, Denise, Mencheres and Kira, they begin the dangerous mission to find their friends and finally put an end to this creep.<br/><br/>I put off reading this long enough, dragging my feet, knowing this is the last book in the series. It was time for the series to</span>
  <span id="freeText7755359368284985489" style="display:none">Don contacts Cat &amp; Bones when he can't find or reach his old team (Tate, Juan, Dave and Cooper). They've been out of communication for weeks so it doesn't take long for them to connect their disappearance to Madigan. With the assistance of Ian, Spade, Denise, Mencheres and Kira, they begin the dangerous mission to find their friends and finally put an end to this creep.<br /><br />I put off reading this long enough, dragging my feet, knowing this is the last book in the series. It was time for the series to end but I've enjoyed them so saying farewell was a little hard. <br /><br />This story met or surpassed my expectations in every regard, even after a little slow start. There were some of the old expected skirmishes but blended in with some surprises, twists and unexpected turns. I like how it ended, even though it was bittersweet. And, there seems to be a huge door open for that much clamored for book starring Ian! I loved the story and it was a fitting end to a thoroughly enjoyable series. 4.5 stars</span>

<div id="review_251713320" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/251713320" />
    <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews"><img alt="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485279859p2/5205999.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/251713320?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️" href="/user/show/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews">❤️ Dorsey aka Wrath Lover Reviews ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781467666329" href="/book/show/18983990-up-from-the-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=audio_books">audio_books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5205999-dorsey-aka-wrath-lover-reviews?shelf=jeaniene_frost">jeaniene_frost</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer251713320" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1885288348737430326"><i>
  <b>** 5 Bittersweet Stars **</b>
</i><br/><br/>Well <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/669810.Jeaniene_Frost' title='Jeaniene Frost' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jeaniene Frost</a> did not disappoint us with the last <i>Night Huntress</i> book!! This book had it all...surprise revelations (one huge one), old friends and allies, and all our favorites from the past. I'm so sad to see this series end!!!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/ogaatWP1024x768_zpsnjtnf9i_edit_1391049037676_zpsozmae6oc.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391056899i/8324638._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo ogaatWP1024x768_zpsnjtnf9i_edit_1391049037676_zpsozmae6oc.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Cat & Bones once again find themselves fighting for survival against powerful forces that want their kind eradicated by causing a war between the Vampires & Ghouls. Evil Madigan plays a part in this but we learn that he is actually </span>
  <span id="freeText1885288348737430326" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>** 5 Bittersweet Stars **</b>
</i><br><br>Well <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/669810.Jeaniene_Frost" title="Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Jeaniene Frost</a> did not disappoint us with the last <i>Night Huntress</i> book!! This book had it all...surprise revelations (one huge one), old friends and allies, and all our favorites from the past. I'm so sad to see this series end!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/ogaatWP1024x768_zpsnjtnf9i_edit_1391049037676_zpsozmae6oc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391056899i/8324638._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ogaatWP1024x768_zpsnjtnf9i_edit_1391049037676_zpsozmae6oc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cat &amp; Bones once again find themselves fighting for survival against powerful forces that want their kind eradicated by causing a war between the Vampires &amp; Ghouls. Evil Madigan plays a part in this but we learn that he is actually working for someone very powerful and it will take Cat, Bones, and all of their formidable allies to win this race war. Don <i>finally</i> reveals his connection to Madigan when he goes to Cat and informes her that Tate, Juan, Dave, and Cooper have disappeared and he fears they're dead, which leads us into the final book.<br><br>What a fantastic end to the series! But it really doesn't feel like the end...maybe wishful thinking but JF definitely left the door open for more. Perhaps sometime down the road she'll revisit and give us more of her wonderful Vampires, Ghouls, and Ghosts.....one can hope.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/UFTG1440x900_zpse3iihay_edit_1391048789119_zpspzmxac8l.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391056899i/8324639._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo UFTG1440x900_zpse3iihay_edit_1391048789119_zpspzmxac8l.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>On a final note...Mrs. Frost has indicated on her website that there will be one more <i>
  <b>Night Huntress World</b>
</i> book. Please, please, please let it be that naughty vamp Ian!!! <i>We need Ian's book!!!</i>…so there you go, something to look forward to along with <i>Vlad's</i> final book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1885288348737430326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_657323905" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/657323905" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/657323905?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer657323905" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18221677570072281703">Since this is the 7th and last book in the series I'm not going to say much because you either love the series by now or you don't.<br/><br/>FYI though I would recommend reading the novella Home for the Holidays before reading this. There is a plot point revealed in that book that is only mentioned briefly in this one.<br/><br/>Leaving a series you love behind is always hard. I have totally enjoyed the entire ride and while I definitely enjoyed some of the books more than the others the journey I’ve taken with Cat </span>
  <span id="freeText18221677570072281703" style="display:none">Since this is the 7th and last book in the series I'm not going to say much because you either love the series by now or you don't.<br /><br />FYI though I would recommend reading the novella Home for the Holidays before reading this. There is a plot point revealed in that book that is only mentioned briefly in this one.<br /><br />Leaving a series you love behind is always hard. I have totally enjoyed the entire ride and while I definitely enjoyed some of the books more than the others the journey I’ve taken with Cat and Bones is one of my favorites. The great thing about the ending of this series is that we get to see almost every character that we have become attached to, they all play a part. Some characters get a little more page time than others but we do get a glimpse of all of them at some point. The whole series wraps up nicely and even though we might see Cat and Bones a little in the future if Ian gets his own book or in Vlad’s final book I felt satisfied with how this series ended and will not be disappointed if they don’t pop up again.<br /><br />Cat and Bones have come full circle. They will fight for each other over every obstacle that is introduced to them. Cat’s old team has gone missing and Don is hiding a terrible secret that he refuses to give up. If Cat is going to save her old team she will have to go to new lengths to find answers. Some of those answers were extremely unexpected.<br /><br />This is an action packed installment with plenty of fighting the bad guys. Cat and Bones are in epic form and prove how much one will go through for the love of their life. There were moments I teared up and moments I smiled. Ian was in rare form this book and I wonder if there will ever be a book and a love interest to tame his wild adventurous spirit. Denise is our go to girl for many of the most trying fights, I guess it is good to have a demon infused human on your side. There is even a respite to Vlad’s wedding for any of you who missed that in his book.<br /><br />The story is faced paced and even though I didn’t see where it was going to end up, I really should have. It was a great ending to a wonderful series that I’m sure I’ll read through again someday.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18221677570072281703" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_315083114" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/315083114" />
    <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library"><img alt="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350750103p2/4551536.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/315083114?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library">Maja (The Nocturnal Library)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=are-you-kidding-me">are-you-kidding-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=failed-to-impress">failed-to-impress</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=i-see-dead-people">i-see-dead-people</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=demons-can-be-hot-too">demons-can-be-hot-too</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=glistening-fangs">glistening-fangs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=reviewed-in-2014">reviewed-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=just-another-book-crush">just-another-book-crush</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer315083114" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11226756934411824433">The ending of a series isn’t necessarily a bad thing, even if it is a well-beloved one. Sometimes, the timing is just right, and with Cat and Bones, it was already a bit overdue. These strong and passionate characters had very little left to give, it was time to put them to rest. <br/><br/>The Night Huntress series was always a rare treat – halfway between urban fantasy and paranormal romance, it had the best of both genres. The first few books were simply fabulous, action-packed, often funny and steaming</span>
  <span id="freeText11226756934411824433" style="display:none">The ending of a series isn’t necessarily a bad thing, even if it is a well-beloved one. Sometimes, the timing is just right, and with Cat and Bones, it was already a bit overdue. These strong and passionate characters had very little left to give, it was time to put them to rest. <br><br>The Night Huntress series was always a rare treat – halfway between urban fantasy and paranormal romance, it had the best of both genres. The first few books were simply fabulous, action-packed, often funny and steaming hot. Frost’s biggest strength is her sense of humor, but she also writes fabulous romances and her secondary characters are always fleshed out and memorable, a fact proven by her three very successful spin-offs. <br><br>However, with the fourth installment, the series clearly started losing its steam, and the last two were almost embarrassingly bad. Yes, I read them solely because I was eager to reunite with the characters, but the disappointments kept piling up and it was clear to me that Frost was a bit tired of this story arc. <br><br>Up from the Grave unfortunately offers more of the same. It is finally time to face Madigan, a strong enemy from the previous two books, under the threat of an all-out war. Cat has a huge personal investment this time, and she fights for her race, her friends and her family. The action scenes were always one of Frost’s strengths, and yet in Up from the Grave, the action seemed almost cartoonish. In fact Frost herself (in Cat’s voice) compares the biggest fight scene to a cartoon. Another thing that bothered me immensely was the repetitiveness. There was a great emotional, almost devastating moment earlier in the series which was basically repeated in Up from the Grave, with similar results. As heartbreaking as it was the first time around, this time, the outcome was pretty clear from the start, and I was mostly bored and severely annoyed. <br><br>Now, I love and need my happily ever after as much as the next girl, especially after seven installments, when I care about the characters so much it hurts. But believe it or not, there is such a thing as a too perfect ending, when things align to give the protagonists (and everyone else) something no one even dreamed about. One of these was served to us on a silver platter in this book, and while it was emotionally satisfying, the rational part of me was quite unhappy. <br><br>Nevertheless, after years of following this series, it was nice to say a proper goodbye. I do hope we’ll see more of Cat and Bones, in spin-offs or novellas, but I’m perfectly happy even if we don’t. I was more than ready to part ways with them.<br><br><br><a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11226756934411824433" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3508102459" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3508102459" />
    <a title="Woman Reading" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/101060033-woman-reading"><img alt="Woman Reading" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565479291p2/101060033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3508102459?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Woman Reading" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Woman Reading" href="/user/show/101060033-woman-reading">Woman Reading</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/101060033-woman-reading?shelf=3-stars-mildly-entertaining">3-stars-mildly-entertaining</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/101060033-woman-reading?shelf=read-women-2020-challenge">read-women-2020-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/101060033-woman-reading?shelf=fantasy-urban-fantasy">fantasy-urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3508102459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15616666286951596325"><b>3☆ the finale of the Cat and Bones' show</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> I’m on the clock here. Besides, I thought you’d like this. There’s a True Blood panel starting soon.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br/>The entire Night Huntress series has reminded me of the last few years of HBO's "True Blood" - for its campiness, casual bloody gore, humor, and later its politics.<br/><br/>Introduced in the previous book, Madigan, the government spook, returns in force in this finale installment. He wants Cat to resume government service while Don alerts her to the sus</span>
  <span id="freeText15616666286951596325" style="display:none"><b>3☆ the finale of the Cat and Bones' show</b><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> I’m on the clock here. Besides, I thought you’d like this. There’s a True Blood panel starting soon.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br />The entire Night Huntress series has reminded me of the last few years of HBO's "True Blood" - for its campiness, casual bloody gore, humor, and later its politics.<br /><br />Introduced in the previous book, Madigan, the government spook, returns in force in this finale installment. He wants Cat to resume government service while Don alerts her to the suspiciously long absence of her ex-teammates. But as Cat and Bones face off against their biggest threat to date, they're not alone. All of their vampire allies join them. Despite Cat's rocky introduction to Bones' sire in book #2, Ian plays a much larger role in this book. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I am, after all, irresistible."<br />I couldn't contain my snort. "I resisted you just fine the day we met, or don't you remember me sticking a knife in your chest?"<br />Ian smiled with lazy wickedness. "I remember, but you seem to have forgotten that you kissed me first. And thoroughly enjoyed it."<br />Caught off guard, I flushed. Hey, I'd been celibate for over four years at the time....I wasn't thinking clearly!</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> But the key question is whether Madigan is working alone? This story is packed with action and some predictable plot twists, especially the young character described in the prologue. The villain is a new one for the series. Cat acts impetuously to her detriment. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> Some people were born to be mothers, fathers, inventors, artists, speakers, preachers . . . and then there was me.<br /><br />"Why do you bother, [Bones]? You married a fighter, so stop trying to convince her that the sidelines suit her better.”<br /><br />Then [Bone's] tone hardened. "The most dangerous enemy you've ever faced is yourself, Kitten. I know that even if you won't admit it." </i>
  </b>
</blockquote>Overall, it was a satisfying conclusion despite not feeling entirely original.<br /><br />Here are links to my reviews for the rest of the series - <br /><br />#0.5 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3521352713" rel="nofollow noopener"><i>Reckoning</i> 3 ☆</a><br />#1 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3506778751" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>Halfway to the Grave</i> 2.5 ☆ </a><br />#2 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3507883153" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>One Foot in the Grave</i> almost 3 ☆</a><br />#3 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3507887440" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>At Grave's End</i> 3 ☆</a><br />#4 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3507891054" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>Destined for an Early Grave</i> 3 ☆ </a><br />#5 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3507965594" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>This Side of the Grave</i> 3 ☆</a><br />#6 <a href="https://www.Goodreads.com/review/show/3508032167" rel="nofollow noopener"> <i>One Grave at a Time</i> 3 ☆</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15616666286951596325" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('yeR93vPrCaGiVjJSN1TtEUnBrLR8i/+W1iRa32Chk5P5foriNyi7T0lTVBpGrJyhV2b24TxD7ZPKZ+2bBSVcqg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YjCdBpH+srqaob+bBiGTb+ocJmuFV9hYbXTS5tsn7OtSqmo6VT0AVHGk2dN32eLf9Lt8PsWfyl1xN2WivqMj0g==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer4972568756487122737">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on </span>
  <span id="freeText4972568756487122737" style="display:none">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on the weekends. Aside from writing, Jeaniene enjoys reading, poetry, watching movies with her husband, exploring old cemeteries, spelunking and traveling – by car. Airplanes, children, and cook books frighten her.<br /><br />For information on Jeaniene's books, book trailers, deleted scenes, creature mythology, and more, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jeanienefrost.com">www.jeanienefrost.com</a><br /></span>

I asked with a snort.<br /><br />Ian gave a sigh of exaggerated patience and glanced at Bones.<br /><br />"Being related to her through you is a real trial.&rdquo;</span>
